      142 +async function rerunAgent(agentId, featureOverride, onAgent, s
          +ignal) {

          +m. Run the full pipeline first.');

          +ayer and anything downstream                                  
      152 +  const agentIdx = AGENTS.indexOf(agentDef);

      158 +

          +ntext, onAgent, signal);

          +ontextKey];

● Here's a complete summary of everything built:

  ---
  Final Product — What Was Shipped

  All servers boot clean. Demo pipeline verified: 4 file-ready + 26 agent + 1 
  complete events.

  Workstream A — Live Pipeline Fixed

  - file-ready events now stream incrementally in live mode — tabs appear as
  each agent finishes, not all at once at the end (was a no-op stub)
  - Cancel actually kills the Codex process — AbortController threads from the
  SSE handler down through orchestrator → base-agent → proc.kill()
  - complete→completed status normalization, zero-file agents emit skipped
  - Pattern matching is .endsWith() only — no more false matches

  Workstream B — Apply/Reset Hardened

  - Migration runs inside db.transaction() — atomic, no partial DB state on
  failure
  - Reset discovers table names dynamically from .migration.sql files, no
  hardcoded list
  - Windows EBUSY handled per-file, reports what was skipped instead of crashing
  - Sandbox reload is awaited with a warning field in the response

  Workstream C+D — Studio + Sandbox Polish

  - ErrorBoundary wraps the whole app + Monaco editor — no more white screens
  - SSE error shows a Retry button + accurate error URL
  - lib/agents.js — single source of truth; no more duplicated color maps
  - Cart persists across iframe reloads via localStorage
  - ProductGrid has loading skeletons, error state with Retry
  - FeatureSlot uses exponential backoff retry instead of hardcoded 2s

  Flagship Features

  - E2 Export Slice — "↓ Export Slice (.patch + PR.md)" button after Apply;
  downloads a git apply-able patch + PR description
  - E3 Write-scope guards — isWithinWriteScope() enforced in applier; violations
  blocked and reported
  - E4 Agent Retry — ↺ button on each agent card in ThinkingConsole; re-runs
  only that layer with upstream context preserved
  - E1 Local Folder Connection — agent/target.js + "📂 Connect Folder" in
  header; sandbox is hardwired as default, custom target is opt-in and clearly
  badged

❯ need to develop another app to use in this demo what stack to choose          

  Thought for 2m 24s (ctrl+o to expand)

● Recommendation: Node + Prisma + PostgreSQL

  Here's why it's the best choice for this demo specifically:

  It fits the existing agent architecture perfectly:
  - Agents already generate Node.js (Express patterns, require(), JS syntax) —
  zero prompt rewriting needed for model/routes/frontend layers
  - Prisma migrations (.prisma schema model blocks) look spectacular in Monaco's
  diff viewer — far more impressive than raw SQL
  - The Database Agent prompt just needs one tweak: CREATE TABLE → Prisma model
  block syntax

  Compared to the alternatives:
  - Drizzle — less recognized by hackathon judges, newer, less documentation for
  agents to reference
  - Python + SQLAlchemy — would require completely rewriting all 4 agent prompts
  from scratch (JS → Python, Express → FastAPI/Flask)
  - Prisma + PostgreSQL — production-grade stack that judges respect, and the
  migration diffs are beautiful

  One thing to prep: Update agent/prompts/layer-prompts.js for the new app's
  Database Agent — instead of generating .migration.sql, generate a Prisma
  schema.prisma migration block. The ORM/API/Frontend agents stay the same since
  they're already Node.js.

  For the local folder demo flow:
  1. Build the Prisma app → get it running locally
  2. In Workbench Studio: click "📂 Connect Folder" → point to the new project
  3. Run a synthesis → show agents generating Prisma schema + model + routes +
  React component against a real production app

  That's the "wow" moment for the judges — not just the sandbox toy, but a real
  codebase getting extended by AI agents live.

     JobBoard App — Build Plan

     Context

     Building a Job Board + Applicant Tracker inside dev_studio_v1/app/ as a
     second, production-grade demo target for Workbench Studio's Local Folder
     Connection (E1 flagship). When connected via "📂 Connect Folder", the four
     Workbench Studio agents will extend this real app — adding features like
     "Add a skill endorsement system" or "Add a messaging system" against real
     Prisma migrations, TypeScript repositories, Express routes, and React
     components.

     The app must also stand on its own as an impressive, beautifully-designed
     product.

     Stack (matches PRD exactly):
     - Server: Node.js 20 + Express 5 + Prisma 5 + PostgreSQL + TypeScript
     - Client: React 18 + Vite 5 + TailwindCSS v3 + shadcn/ui + TanStack Query
     v5 + Zustand + React Router v6 + React Hook Form + Zod
     - Auth: JWT access token (15m) + refresh token (7d) with DB-backed rotation

     ---
     Folder Structure

     dev_studio_v1/
     └── app/
         ├── server/                    ← Express API (port 4001 to avoid
     conflict with agent :4000)
         │   ├── prisma/
         │   │   ├── schema.prisma      ← Full schema from PRD §4.3
         │   │   ├── seed.ts            ← Realistic seed: 2 employers, 8 jobs,
     12 candidates, applications
         │   │   └── migrations/        ← Auto-generated by prisma migrate dev
         │   ├── src/
         │   │   ├── index.ts           ← Bootstrap: app.listen(4001)
         │   │   ├── app.ts             ← Express config, cors, helmet, morgan,
     routes mount
         │   │   ├── config/
         │   │   │   └── env.ts         ← Zod-validated env vars
         │   │   ├── middleware/
         │   │   │   ├── auth.ts        ← JWT verify → req.user
         │   │   │   ├── role.ts        ← requireRole(...roles) factory
         │   │   │   ├── validate.ts    ← Zod schema validation wrapper
         │   │   │   └── error.ts       ← Global error handler → {
     success:false, error }
         │   │   ├── prisma/
         │   │   │   ├── client.ts      ← Singleton PrismaClient
         │   │   │   ├── userRepo.ts
         │   │   │   ├── jobRepo.ts
         │   │   │   ├── applicationRepo.ts
         │   │   │   ├── companyRepo.ts
         │   │   │   └── interviewRepo.ts
         │   │   ├── services/
         │   │   │   ├── auth.service.ts        ← bcrypt, JWT sign/verify,
     refresh rotation
         │   │   │   ├── application.service.ts ← Pipeline state machine, status
     validation
         │   │   │   ├── job.service.ts         ← Business logic, close expired
     jobs
         │   │   │   └── email.service.ts       ← Nodemailer (stubbed in dev,

         │   │   │   ├── index.ts        ← Mount all under /api/v1

         │   │   │   ├── job.schema.ts
         │   │   │   ├── application.schema.ts

         │   │       └── apiResponse.ts   ← { success, data, meta, error }

     ---
     Prisma Schema

     Implement exactly as in PRD_JobBoard_Applicant_Tracker.md §4.3. Key models:
     - User (Role: CANDIDATE | EMPLOYER | ADMIN)
     - Company (1:1 with EMPLOYER user)
     - Job (JobType enum, salary range, tags, soft delete via isActive)
     - JobTag (separate table with @@unique([jobId, name]) for indexed tag
     filtering)
     - Application (ApplicationStatus state machine, @@unique([candidateId,
     jobId]))
     - Interview (1:1 with Application, upsert for rescheduling)
     - SavedJob (@@unique([userId, jobId]))
     - RefreshToken (DB-backed rotation, onDelete: Cascade)

     ---
     API Routes (full contract from PRD §6.2)

     Port: 4001 (avoids collision with Workbench Studio agent on :4000)

     All routes under /api/v1. Full route table as per PRD. Key highlights:
     - POST /auth/register → returns user + both tokens
     - PATCH /applications/:id/status → triggers email + state machine
     validation
     - GET /jobs → filters: keyword, type, location, tags[], salaryMin/Max,
     page, limit
     - GET /applications/job/:jobId → employer view with status filter

     Pipeline state machine in application.service.ts:
     APPLIED → SCREENING → INTERVIEW → OFFER → HIRED
                                             → REJECTED (any stage)
     Invalid transitions (e.g. HIRED → SCREENING) return 400.

     ---
     UI Design Direction

     Visual Identity — Professional Dark Theme (confirmed)

     - Palette:
       - Page bg: #0a0f1a (deeper than slate-900 for premium feel)
       - Card surface: #111827 (gray-900)
       - Elevated card: #1a2235
       - Border: #1f2d40
       - Accent primary: #6366f1 (indigo-500), hover #818cf8
       - Accent secondary: #06b6d4 (cyan-500) for highlights
       - Success/HIRED: #10b981 (emerald-500)
       - Text primary: #f1f5f9, secondary: #94a3b8, muted: #475569
       - Gradient hero: linear-gradient(135deg, #0a0f1a 0%, #0f172a 50%, #1a0a2e
     100%)
     - Typography: Inter via Google Fonts — 400/500/600/700/800
     - Radius: rounded-2xl (16px) for hero cards, rounded-xl (12px) cards,
     rounded-lg inputs
     - Shadows: shadow-xl shadow-black/40 for card lift, colored glow on hover
     for job cards
     - Animations: transition-all duration-200 on all interactive elements;
     subtle scale on card hover; shimmer loading skeletons

     Status Badge Colors (ApplicationStatus)

     ┌───────────┬────────────────┬─────────────┐
     │  Status   │   Background   │    Text     │
     ├───────────┼────────────────┼─────────────┤
     │ APPLIED   │ indigo-500/20  │ indigo-300  │
     ├───────────┼────────────────┼─────────────┤
     │ SCREENING │ amber-500/20   │ amber-300   │
     ├───────────┼────────────────┼─────────────┤
     │ INTERVIEW │ blue-500/20    │ blue-300    │
     ├───────────┼────────────────┼─────────────┤
     │ OFFER     │ purple-500/20  │ purple-300  │
     ├───────────┼────────────────┼─────────────┤
     │ HIRED     │ emerald-500/20 │ emerald-300 │
     ├───────────┼────────────────┼─────────────┤
     │ REJECTED  │ red-500/20     │ red-300     │
     └───────────┴────────────────┴─────────────┘

     Key Pages Design

     HomePage (public):
     - Full-width hero: dark gradient bg, large headline "Find your next
     opportunity", search bar
     - Featured company logos strip
     - Stats: "12,000+ Jobs · 800+ Companies · 45,000+ Candidates"
     - Featured job cards (3-column grid)
     - CTA sections for employers and candidates

     JobsPage:
     - Left sidebar (260px): filters (keyword input, job type checkboxes, salary
     slider, tag chips)
     - Right: paginated JobCard grid (2-column)
     - JobCard: company logo avatar, title, company name, location badge,
     salary, type badge, posted date, "Save" bookmark icon

     JobDetailPage:
     - Left: full job description (rich text) + company info
     - Right sticky panel: salary range, type, location, "Apply Now" button,
     deadline countdown

     PipelineBoard (employer):
     - Horizontal Kanban: 6 columns (APPLIED · SCREENING · INTERVIEW · OFFER ·
     HIRED · REJECTED)
     - Each column: count badge, scrollable ApplicantCards
     - ApplicantCard: avatar, name, applied date, interview badge if scheduled
     - Click card → slide-over drawer with full application detail + status
     dropdown + note field

     Candidate Dashboard:
     - Stats row: Applied (n), Screening (n), Interviews (n), Offers (n)
     - Application timeline cards: company logo, job title, status badge,
     last-updated
     - Saved jobs section below

     Employer Dashboard:
     - Stats: total jobs posted, total applicants, active listings, hired this
     month
     - Recent applicants table
     - Quick-post job CTA card

     Login / Register:
     - Split-screen: left = illustration/brand, right = form
     - RegisterPage: role toggle (Candidate / Employer) at top of form
     - Clean inputs with labels above, inline Zod validation errors

     ---
     Seed Data

     prisma/seed.ts generates:
     - 2 Employer users + their Company profiles (TechCorp, StartupHub)
     - 1 Admin user
     - 5 Candidate users
     - 8 Jobs across both companies (mix of FULL_TIME, REMOTE, CONTRACT,
     INTERNSHIP)
     - 15 Applications in various pipeline stages (to fill the Kanban board)
     - 3 Interviews scheduled
     - Some saved jobs

     All passwords = Password123! for easy demo login.

     ---
     Build Order (sequential phases)

     Phase 1 — Server foundation

     1. app/server/package.json (deps: express, @types/express, prisma,
     @prisma/client, zod, bcryptjs, jsonwebtoken, cors, helmet, morgan,
     nodemailer, ts-node, typescript, tsx, nodemon)
     2. app/server/tsconfig.json
     3. app/server/prisma/schema.prisma (full schema from PRD)
     4. app/server/.env (DATABASE_URL, JWT secrets, PORT=4001)
     5. app/server/src/config/env.ts
     6. app/server/src/prisma/client.ts
     7. app/server/src/utils/ (jwt.ts, hash.ts, pagination.ts, apiResponse.ts)
     8. All repository files (userRepo.ts, jobRepo.ts, etc.)
     9. app/server/src/services/auth.service.ts
     10. app/server/src/services/application.service.ts (state machine)
     11. app/server/src/services/job.service.ts
     12. app/server/src/services/email.service.ts (stub with console.log in dev)
     13. All Zod schemas (auth.schema.ts, job.schema.ts, etc.)
     14. All middleware (auth.ts, role.ts, validate.ts, error.ts)
     15. All controllers + routes
     16. app/server/src/app.ts + app/server/src/index.ts
     17. app/server/prisma/seed.ts

     Phase 2 — Client foundation

     1. app/client/package.json (deps: react, react-dom, react-router-dom,
     @tanstack/react-query, zustand, axios, react-hook-form,
     @hookform/resolvers, zod, lucide-react, clsx, tailwind-merge)
     2. app/client/vite.config.ts (proxy: /api → http://localhost:4001)
     3. app/client/tailwind.config.ts + components.json (shadcn/ui dark theme)
     4. app/client/src/types/ (all type files)
     5. app/client/src/lib/ (queryClient.ts, utils.ts)
     6. app/client/src/store/auth.store.ts
     7. app/client/src/api/axios.ts (interceptors with token refresh)
     8. All src/api/*.ts files
     9. All src/hooks/*.ts files

     Phase 3 — UI components + pages

     1. Global CSS + shadcn/ui setup (Button, Badge, Input, Modal, Spinner,
     Pagination)
     2. Layout components (Navbar, Sidebar, Footer)
     3. Auth pages (LoginPage, RegisterPage)
     4. Public pages (HomePage, JobsPage, JobDetailPage, CompanyPage)
     5. Candidate pages (DashboardPage, ApplicationsPage, ProfilePage)
     6. Employer pages (DashboardPage, MyJobsPage, PostJobPage, PipelinePage,
     CompanySettingsPage)
     7. Guards (AuthGuard, RoleGuard)
     8. App.tsx (all routes wired)

     ---
     Environment Setup Notes

     Prerequisites the user must have:
     - PostgreSQL running locally (or via Docker: docker run -e 
     POSTGRES_PASSWORD=postgres -p 5432:5432 postgres)
     - DATABASE_URL=postgresql://postgres:postgres@localhost:5432/jobboard

     After implementation, run:
     cd app/server
     npx prisma migrate dev --name init
     npx prisma db seed
     npm run dev            # :4001

     # separate terminal
     cd app/client
     npm run dev            # :5173

     ---
     Workbench Studio Integration

     Once the app runs, demo the Local Folder Connection:
     1. In Studio header → "📂 Connect Folder" → <absolute 
     path>/dev_studio_v1/app/server
     2. Layer map: DB → prisma/schema.prisma area, ORM → src/prisma/, API →
     src/routes/ + src/controllers/, UI → ../client/src/components/
     3. Synthesize "Add a skill endorsement system" → agents generate Prisma
     model + repository + route + React component against the real JobBoard
     codebase

     ---
     Verification

     1. cd app/server && npx prisma migrate dev && npm run dev → server starts
     on :4001 with no errors
     2. GET http://localhost:4001/api/v1/jobs → returns seeded jobs array
     3. POST /api/v1/auth/register + POST /api/v1/auth/login → returns tokens
     4. Authenticated POST /api/v1/jobs as EMPLOYER → creates job
     5. PATCH /api/v1/applications/:id/status with HIRED → returns 200; invalid
     transition → 400
     6. cd app/client && npm run dev → opens at :5173
     7. JobsPage renders 8 seeded jobs with filters working
     8. Register as Candidate → apply to a job → application appears in employer
     pipeline
     9. Employer drags applicant to INTERVIEW → InterviewScheduler modal opens
     10. Connect to Studio Local Folder → synthesize a new feature → agents
     produce files in the right directories
